*!
!* '''When'''  MSTR report is executed and MSTR produced a csv file
!*> Execute MSTR report
|com.objectmentor.fixtures.CommandLineFixture|
|command|ssh -tt -i ${bastionkey} -o !-StrictHostKeyChecking=no-! ${mstrServer} 'bash -s' << EOF  sleep 5;sudo /opt/MicroStrategy/bin/mstrsysmgr -w /home/genesaas/runTest.smw -p user=administrator password= project=${dbname}; exit;EOF|
*!
!*> '''And''' Copy file from MSTR server to DbFit Server and Load csv file into postgres DB [local instance]
|com.objectmentor.fixtures.CommandLineFixture|
|command               |sleep 25              |

|com.objectmentor.fixtures.CommandLineFixture|
|command|mstr-script/copy-file.sh ${dbname} ${mstrServer} ApplicationsPending_Decisions_Dataset2.csv|
*!
!*> Capture source data
!include .SaasBiTest.CreateFunction
*!
*!

!* '''Then''' Compare the data on source and target
!*> Drop table if exists
!|Execute|DROP TABLE IF EXISTS dbfit_test.app_pending3 CASCADE|

|commit|
*!
!*> Load CSV file into DB
!|Execute|!- set schema 'dbfit_test' -!|

!|Execute|!- 
DO $$ BEGIN
      PERFORM "load_csv_file2"('app_pending3','/home/jenkins/workspace/-!${dbname}!-/ApplicationsPending_Decisions_Dataset2.csv',8);
END $$;

-!|

|commit|
*!
!*> Microstrategy Data (Target Data)
!|Store Query|!- select count (distinct application_number)::integer no_of_refer_apps
,date::date date1
from dbfit_test.app_pending3
group by date
order by date
 -!|target_data|

*!

!* Compare source data with target data
!*< Setup
!|dbfit.PostgresTest                       |
!|ConnectUsingFile|${env} |
|set option|bind symbols|false|
*!
!*> Source Query
!|Store Query|!- select count (distinct applicationnumber)::integer no_of_refer_apps
, dt.datename::date date1
from
(
select applicationnumber,producttype, applicationcreationtimestamp,applicationupdatetimestamp,decisiontype,"Pst-B-Policy-Decision-Category",applicationupdatelocaldatekey
,rank() OVER (PARTITION BY applicationnumber ORDER BY applicationupdatetimestamp DESC) rnk
from public.f_application_decision
) a
inner join d_date dt on dt.datepk = a.applicationupdatelocaldatekey 
where a.rnk=1
and lower(decisiontype)='system' and
"Pst-B-Policy-Decision-Category" = 'Refer'
group by dt.datename 
order by datename
 -!|source_data|

|commit|
*!

|compare stored queries|source_data|target_data| 
|no_of_refer_apps|date1|
*!
*!
